SUBENT        V1002001   20160402                             V034V100200100001 
BIB                 10         38                                 V100200100002 
TITLE      Atlas of neutron resonances resonance parameters and   V100200100003 
            thermal cross sections Z=1-100                        V100200100004 
AUTHOR     (S.F.Mughabghab)                                       V100200100005 
INSTITUTE  (1USABNL)                                              V100200100006 
REFERENCE  (B,NEUT.RES,,2006)                                     V100200100007 
REL-REF    (E,,S.F.Mughabghab+,B,NEUT.CS 1A,,1981)                V100200100008 
           (E,,S.F.Mughabghab,B,NEUT.CS 1B,,1984)                 V100200100009 
           (O,V1001001,S.F.Mughabghab,B,NEUT.RES,,2006)           V100200100010 
           First part of the compilation from the same book       V100200100011 
METHOD     Evaluation: The experimental results for nuclei        V100200100012 
            between H and Fm were critically surveyed,            V100200100013 
            renormalized and resonance parameters were deduced.   V100200100014 
           Cross sections and resonance integrals were given      V100200100015 
            where available, otherwise they were calculated using V100200100016 
            the resonance parameter data.                         V100200100017 
ANALYSIS   Resonance parameters and cross sections were analyzed  V100200100018 
            using Atlas codes.                                    V100200100019 
           The neutron radiative cross sections were measured in  V100200100020 
            a Maxwellian flux, other measurements are commented.  V100200100021 
           Scattering length (coherent amplitude) b is related to V100200100022 
            elastic scattering cross section as follows:          V100200100023 
             sigma=4pi x b**2.                                    V100200100024 
            Both values are based on independent measurements.    V100200100025 
           Resonance integrals (RI) are based on experimental     V100200100026 
            values, if no measurements then calculated from       V100200100027 
            resonance parameter values from 0.5 eV to highest     V100200100028 
            energy of the resolved resonance region.              V100200100029 
ERR-ANALYS (ERR-T) S.F. Mughabghab tabulated total errors for     V100200100030 
            integral values.                                      V100200100031 
ADD-RES    The Atlas also contains vast resonance parameter data, V100200100032 
            however, it is next to impossible to compile it       V100200100033 
            manually and Elsevier copyright agreement prevents    V100200100034 
            any usage of electronic files.                        V100200100035
